   <script type="text/javascript">
    function catchOutboundClick(link) {
      link.onclick = function(e){
        trackOutboundLink(link, "Outbound Links", link.hostname);
      }
  }

  function trackOutboundLink(link, category, action) {
    try {
      ga('send', {
        'hitType': 'event',
        'eventCategory': category,
        'eventAction': action
      });
    } catch(err){}
  }

  var outRe = new RegExp('^http:\/\/.+$','i');
  var inRe = new RegExp('^http:\/\/'+location.hostname.replace("www.", "")+'.+$','i');
  var links = document.getElementsByTagName("a");

  for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
    var link = links[i];
    if (outRe.test(link.href) && !inRe.test(link.href)){
      catchOutboundClick(link);
    }
  }
   </script>
